    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

        if (this.up('#box')) {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: $('box').getStyle('z-index')})});
        } else {

          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });

<span id="freeTextContainer16570712155068919995">When thirty-year-old English teacher Anna Emerson is offered a job tutoring T.J. Callahan at his family's summer rental in the Maldives, she accepts without hesitation; a working vacation on a tropical island trumps the library any day.<br/><br/>T.J. Callahan has no desire to leave town, not that anyone asked him. He's almost seventeen and if having cancer wasn't bad enough, now he </span>
  <span id="freeText16570712155068919995" style="display:none">When thirty-year-old English teacher Anna Emerson is offered a job tutoring T.J. Callahan at his family's summer rental in the Maldives, she accepts without hesitation; a working vacation on a tropical island trumps the library any day.<br /><br />T.J. Callahan has no desire to leave town, not that anyone asked him. He's almost seventeen and if having cancer wasn't bad enough, now he has to spend his first summer in remission with his family—and a stack of overdue assignments—instead of his friends.<br /><br />Anna and T.J. are en route to join T.J.'s family in the Maldives when the pilot of their seaplane suffers a fatal heart attack and crash-lands in the Indian Ocean. Adrift in shark-infested waters, their life jackets keep them afloat until they make it to the shore of an uninhabited island. Now Anna and T.J. just want to survive and they must work together to obtain water, food, fire, and shelter.<br /><br />Their basic needs might be met but as the days turn to weeks, and then months, the castaways encounter plenty of other obstacles, including violent tropical storms, the many dangers lurking in the sea, and the possibility that T.J.'s cancer could return. As T.J. celebrates yet another birthday on the island, Anna begins to wonder if the biggest challenge of all might be living with a boy who is gradually becoming a man.</span>

<div id="review_271021869" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/271021869" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/271021869?book_show_action=true">Feb 01, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781466363212" href="/book/show/12991245-on-the-island">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=6-star-books">6-star-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer271021869" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9324194465508966839">Wow. 5.5 stars!! (New review - edited after re-read)<br/><br/><b> LOVE LOVE LOVED this absolutely <i> beautiful </i>, unique and unforgettable story about survival and love. </b><br/><br/>Its well-written, riveting and heartfelt. The HEA ending is just perfect with an epilogue that brought the happiest tears to my eyes. I honestly don’t have one single complaint to make about the this book.<br/><br/>One of my top favorite reads ever!<br/><br/>I just finished reading it for the second time. I read it once a year ago and absolutely adored it but it w</span>
  <span id="freeText9324194465508966839" style="display:none">Wow. 5.5 stars!! (New review - edited after re-read)<br><br><b> LOVE LOVE LOVED this absolutely <i> beautiful </i>, unique and unforgettable story about survival and love. </b><br><br>Its well-written, riveting and heartfelt. The HEA ending is just perfect with an epilogue that brought the happiest tears to my eyes. I honestly don’t have one single complaint to make about the this book.<br><br>One of my top favorite reads ever!<br><br>I just finished reading it for the second time. I read it once a year ago and absolutely adored it but it was in my pre-review writing days and so, now that I’ve re-read it, I just wanted to tell you all how much I absolutely adored this story.<br><br>Its one of those stories that reminds you that true love can be found in the least likely of places and that, no matter what other people think, you should always follow your heart.<br><br>When an unfortunate plane crash strands them together on a small uninhabited island in the Maldives, 16-year-old TJ, a high school student in remission from cancer, and his 30-year-old summer tutor Anna are forced to depend on each other for survival as they wait to be rescued.<br>And wait.<br>And wait and wait and wait.<br>Weeks turn to months and eventually to years with no sign of rescue on the horizon.<br>But as their time on the island passes, Anna is faced with the reality that the boy she came to the island with is now becoming a man.<br><br>First of all you need to know that TJ isn’t like most other teens. He feels about twice as old as he is. Seriously, when you ‘meet’ him, you’ll understand. The events of his life have matured him far beyond his years and he so incredibly sure of his feelings that it is guaranteed to melt your heart.<br><br>For those of you who are wondering if the age difference makes their relationship feel at all weird, I promise, it <u> absolutely </u> does <b> not </b> . Cross my heart. They don’t get physically involved until he is almost 19-years-old so there is never an ‘underage’ issue. Watching them slowly fall for each other as he got much older was beautifully written, plausibly paced and never rushed. And if you read the book, you’ll see without question that they really, truly belong together.<br><br><i> <b> “I love you, Anna.”<br>The surprised look on her face told me she hadn’t seen that coming.<br>“You weren’t supposed to fall in love,” she whispered.<br>“Well, I did,” I said, looking into her eyes. “I’ve been in love with you for months. I’m telling you now because I think you love me too, Anna. You just don’t think you’re supposed to. You’ll tell me when you’re ready. I can wait.” </b></i> <br><br>The author is a brilliantly gifted story-teller who perfectly captures and portrays intensity of the situation that Anna and TJ went though – depending on each other, supporting each other, saving each other.<br><br>The book is told in alternating chapter POV’s between Anna and TJ. It is done very seamlessly allowing the reader a chance to really get into the minds of both the main character – something vital given the nature of the storyline.<br><br>Its one of those incredibly written books that you never want to put down – where you are immersed in the story and connected to the characters right from the beginning.<br><br>Another thing that you should know is that TJ’s cancer does not come back. This not a story about that. I’ve heard some people say that that held them back from wanting to read this book so I’d like to dispel that worry here. This is a beautiful love story with a very <b> happy </b> ending!!<br><br><i> <b> "I kissed her as soon as we were inside her apartment, and I wasn’t gentle about it, holding her face firmly in my hands and pressing my lips hard against hers. She wasn’t anyone’s to own – I knew that – but right then she was mine.” </b></i> <br><br><br>If you haven’t yet read it, trust me, its worth bumping to the very top of your lists!!<br><br>I know I’ll be rereading it many times for years to come &lt;3<br><br>CASTING:<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380751798i/3119537._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="9324194465508966839" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2485843857" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2485843857" />
    <a title="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments"><img alt="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554228831p2/67920559.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2485843857?book_show_action=true">Sep 04, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰" href="/user/show/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments">Alex ✰ Comets and Comments ✰</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=forbidden-fruit">forbidden-fruit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=guilty-pleasures">guilty-pleasures</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=recommended-to-me">recommended-to-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=slow-burn">slow-burn</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=better-late-than-never">better-late-than-never</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=cute-and-cuddly">cute-and-cuddly</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/67920559-alex-comets-and-comments?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2485843857" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10908778687225007786"><i>
  <b>“It would always be summer on the island.”</b>
</i><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1536085318ra/26252582.gif' width='600' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b><br/>This was such a warm book hug *heart eyes* </b><br/>_____________<br/><br/><u>
  <b>The Plot</b>
</u><br/>I'm late to the love for this book. <br/><i>On The Island</i> has been on my tbr for the longest of time for one thing and one thing only; the premise. The story that Graves writes is so one-of-a-kind and unique (which is pretty hard to find in the Romance genre) that it begs it's readers to give it a go. <br/><br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I don't fit in your world."<br/>"Neither do I," he said, his expression tender yet reso</blockquote></b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText10908778687225007786" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>“It would always be summer on the island.”</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1536085318ra/26252582.gif" width="600" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><br>This was such a warm book hug *heart eyes* </b><br>_____________<br><br><u>
  <b>The Plot</b>
</u><br>I'm late to the love for this book. <br><i>On The Island</i> has been on my tbr for the longest of time for one thing and one thing only; the premise. The story that Graves writes is so one-of-a-kind and unique (which is pretty hard to find in the Romance genre) that it begs it's readers to give it a go. <br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I don't fit in your world."<br>"Neither do I," he said, his expression tender yet resolute. "So let's make our own. We've done it before.” </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br>Anna Emerson is a thirty year old teacher that flies to the Maldives with her summer tutor student - seventeen year old T.J Callahan. Packing her bags and leaving behind her boyfriend, John she hopes on a plane with her whole summer planned. <br><br>When they find out they have to take a sea plane into the island, their plans get changed. Then when the pilot suffers from cardiac arrest, both T.J and Anna realize that they're about to crash land in the middle of the ocean. (Re-writing the plot for this, makes me want to dive right back into it... pun intended) <br><br>Anna and T.J survive the crash but have to learn to survive in isolation on an island. All they have are the clothes on their backs and each other. The story follows their fight for survival, it is a coming of age in the sense both characters develop in different manners. Stuck on an island, learning how to find food, water and shelter is hard enough... and as nobody seems to be coming and saving them - they build a trust too. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1536086576ra/26252665.gif" width="600" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Don’t let go,” I whispered.<br>“I wasn’t going to.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br><br><br><u>
  <b>Little Gems</b>
</u><br>There was so much packed into this book. <br>Humor, love, survival, grief, growing up... It was such a wonderful treat to sit down with some chocolates and just escape. Although, the writing was mediocre - the author really does a good job with imagery and you end up being on the island with Anna and T.J. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1536086576ra/26252664.gif" width="600" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I read this in one sitting and it was like having a hot chocolate on a cold wintry night. This review seriously is filled with so many chocolate references... I guess, that should really just prove how I enjoyed it! <br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I woke up with a hard-on.<br>I usually did, and it wasn’t like I had any control over it. Now that we weren’t almost dead, my body must have decided all systems were a go. ”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br>One thing I enjoyed was the humor through the tragic. T.J is a cancer patient and their situation is so fragile. The pacing and the timing for when their bond started to form into friendship and later more, was so perfectly planned. It didn't feel too fast or too slow. I was skeptical about how the writer would pull of the age gap (also cheers for showing that women can be older too!) but it was done so meticulously!<br><br>I wish I read this sooner and during the time my GR friends did. I would have loved to seen the hype for this grow and see more and more people fall in love on the island &lt;3 <br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“You named the chicken, Chicken?" <br>She looked embarrassed. "When we decided not to kill it, I got attached.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="10908778687225007786" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1053760-shelby-trains-flying-monkeys?shelf=made-my-face-rain">made-my-face-rain</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1053760-shelby-trains-flying-monkeys?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447374454ra/16995422.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Anna is a thirty year old teacher who has agreed to tutor a 17 year old that has recently gone into remission from cancer. The treatments caused him to get behind at school so his family decides to spend the summer with a tutor to catch him up. This family has some cash though so they are headed to their summer rental in the Maldives.<br>The family has already left leaving Anna and her student TJ to join them. The small plane that is taking them to join the family though has some problems and the pilot ends up having an heart attack during the trip. Their plane crashes.<br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447374454ra/16995423.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Anna and TJ end up shipwrecked together, hoping that a rescue plane is on the way.<br>I LOVE THESE KINDS OF STORIES!! They must find some way to survive on the island, no water, no food. <br>Just each other.<br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447374454ra/16995424.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>TJ and Anna have to battle not only the weather, sharks and so many other natural problems. They also have always in the backs of their minds that his cancer could come back.<br><br>Now I'm sure you are going to read some reviews that say that this book wasn't the best written piece of literature, but so what? I LOVED it. Sometimes you just want someone to tell you a story, and this author does it well. There is no insta-love. These two built a history together slowly. Anna is torn about the way she begins to feel about TJ because of his age. (Don't say anything here, because I'm older than my husband and went through some of the same misgivings that Anna did). Their story builds like it should, and it's damn fabulous.<br>AND:<br> The book earned one whole star for mentioning the bestest movie ever!<br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Now I'm going to go and smooch my younger husband and enjoy ever second of it. Because us older women have some swag too.<br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2020017469?book_show_action=true">Jun 04, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2020017469" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3228753720252996306"><br/><br/>5 <b>Unique, Unforgettable & Unputdownable!!</b> Stars!!!<br/><br/>I went in totally blind, and so thrilled I did. I had no preconceived notions about what I was going to read except that a really great Goodreads friend, Robin, gave it five stars months ago, and I immediately added it to my tbr. I honestly forgot about it until this same great friend gifted this book to me a couple of days ago. I thought, "Yeah, I am definitely in the mood for an island getaway, which I am sure involves romance." I am so glad I </span>
  <span id="freeText3228753720252996306" style="display:none"><br /><br />5 <b>Unique, Unforgettable &amp; Unputdownable!!</b> Stars!!!<br /><br />I went in totally blind, and so thrilled I did. I had no preconceived notions about what I was going to read except that a really great Goodreads friend, Robin, gave it five stars months ago, and I immediately added it to my tbr. I honestly forgot about it until this same great friend gifted this book to me a couple of days ago. I thought, "Yeah, I am definitely in the mood for an island getaway, which I am sure involves romance." I am so glad I didn't read the blurb or re-read my friend's review. I was absolutely blown away! And I think you will be too. <br /><br />Here is the slightest of teases, again hoping you will mainly go in blind and be mesmerized by this story and it's characters .....<br /><br />On board a seaplane hopping from one island of The Maldives to their destination island two hours away, it crashes into the Indian Ocean, due to the pilot dying before the plane ever hits the water. Luckily before the heart attack claimed the pilot's life, he instructed his two passengers to put on their life jackets and buckle up.<br /><br />Minutes before boarding a plane with a sixteen year old boy she would be tutoring for the summer, named T.J., who was also in remission from Hodgin's lymphoma, Anna says her goodbye to her boyfriend of eight years. John tells her he loves her and not to make any final decisions until she gets back. Anna is a sophomore English teacher and is spending the next couple of months with T.J. and his parents, on an island in the middle of the Indian Ocean. His parents already arrived to their destination spot a few days prior. Anna, thirty years old, has a big decision to make. Will she continue to stay with John when she arrives back in the states, or would her life be better without him in it?<br /><br />Okay ...... that is all the background info you get out of this gal. Hopefully it is a good enough tease, because I sincerely encourage you all to read this one. I literally could not put it down once I started. It was riveting and one I will never forget. The storyline is so fascinating, unique and extremely well written. <br /><br /> <b>
  <i>"Is your life better with him, Anna, or without him?"</i>
</b><br /><br />	◦	<br /></span>

<div id="review_276502974" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/276502974" />
    <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p"><img alt="♡Karlyn P♡" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1389996373p2/1131400.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/276502974?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♡Karlyn P♡" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p">♡Karlyn P♡</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/12586192-on-the-island">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=steam-warm">steam-warm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=read-2012">read-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=genre-contemporary">genre-contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer276502974" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11537063720911223667"><br/><b>Awesome, awesome, awesome! </b><br/><br/>wow, what a great book this turned out to be! It's one of the few 'hyped' books I've read lately that really live up to the hype. <br/><br/>At first I really wasn't sure about it. The book description didn't sound like my cuppa, and in a way it wasn't, but the author really made this one work and made me a believer. <br/><br/>Seriously, don't shy away from this one! Yes, there is a whopping age difference between the H/h, with the heroine being the older of the two. 13 1/2 years actually,</span>
  <span id="freeText11537063720911223667" style="display:none"><br /><b>Awesome, awesome, awesome! </b><br /><br />wow, what a great book this turned out to be! It's one of the few 'hyped' books I've read lately that really live up to the hype. <br /><br />At first I really wasn't sure about it. The book description didn't sound like my cuppa, and in a way it wasn't, but the author really made this one work and made me a believer. <br /><br />Seriously, don't shy away from this one! Yes, there is a whopping age difference between the H/h, with the heroine being the older of the two. 13 1/2 years actually, but <b>by the time the romance happens they were both equal in all ways important: two fully grown adults living alone with the barest resources for their creature comfort and survival, and no longer believing in ever joining the real world again. Under those circumstances, the romance really worked. </b><br /><br />The author never cheapens the romance either, it is of the heart and not meant to just titillate the reader. Nothing smutty or milf'y about it. Just an odd but beautiful love.<br /><br />This story is a self published indie book, so yes it has some rough spots. But the author will quickly suck you into the story with her writing. This entire story is told from both the hero and heroine's POV. It switches off from her first-person accounts, to his first-person accounts, and back and forth. LOVED IT!! <br /><br />There was so much to enjoy in this book. Great chemistry and characters, loved the survival aspect, and no sugar coating their dire situation. It made an emotional and gripping read. Oh boy did I cry in a few places too! <br /><br />Thanks everyone who recommended it!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11537063720911223667" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781466363212" href="/book/show/12991245-on-the-island">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5918467-calia?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer253677831" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2852094603412559355">Before I even start my review I need to ask the most important question..... <br/>How is this Tracey’s first book? I’m skeptical, I don’t believe it. <br/>She writes so flawlessly. <br/>The story was <b>amazing</b>! <br/><br/>I mean, she wrote about two people living on a island, how entertaining could that possibly be? <br/>Turns out more than I knew.. <i>I truly could not stop reading this book.</i> <br/><br/>I read this during a nasty cold. Now thats dedication people! <br/><br/>T.J. is a sixteen year old, that is in remission from cancer. Anna is a 30 ye</span>
  <span id="freeText2852094603412559355" style="display:none">Before I even start my review I need to ask the most important question..... <br />How is this Tracey’s first book? I’m skeptical, I don’t believe it. <br />She writes so flawlessly. <br />The story was <b>amazing</b>! <br /><br />I mean, she wrote about two people living on a island, how entertaining could that possibly be? <br />Turns out more than I knew.. <i>I truly could not stop reading this book.</i> <br /><br />I read this during a nasty cold. Now thats dedication people! <br /><br />T.J. is a sixteen year old, that is in remission from cancer. Anna is a 30 year old teacher that is hired by his parents to tutor him over the summer. The family is vacationing in the Maldives. But when T.J and Anna fly overseas, on the last end of their trip, their pilot suffers a heartattack, and the plane goes down. <br /><br />Neither are prepared (but who really would be?) for the challenges that are ahead of them.<br /><br />This is where I became hooked to this book! <br />Every action, discovery, triumph, and loss T.J and Anna went through on the island had me captivated. <br /><br />When I read the book, I felt like a lard ass. <br />I’m lounging around the house drinking water. I probably made a sandwich. Meanwhile, they’d cut off a limb for a simple glass of water, and a freakin' taco! <br />It makes you grateful for everything around you, and shows you just how much resolve and determination we all have (but don’t know) when it comes to survival. <br /><br />It’s hard for me to even believe that I would get THIS into On the Island. As a kid, my parents made me watch <i>Castaway</i> and I almost lost the will to live. To this day I still cringe over that damn ball, Wilson. <br /><br />But when Anna found the chicken and named him Chicken, and made the animal her "pet", I could understand it...<br /><br />To the romance. <br />You’re skeptical. <br />Heck, I was. I mean the age difference is vast. So you think it would be odd, maybe even awkward. <br /><br />Their situation brought them together and created a bond that no one else could understand. The romance to this story was inevitable. I need to stress, its not awkward. <b>Not.At. All.</b><br /><br />I mean, can we blame Anna? <br />As T.J. grows up into a man, I have to say I wouldn’t have been apposed to him either. In fact I was a little jealous she was stranded with him. <br /><br />But I liked that Anna was conscious of the age difference. She tried to fight her feelings, and it gave the book a realistic vibe. <br />Yet, when Anna gives in to her feelings. If I knew how to fist pump, I think I would have at that moment....<br /><br />The irony is not lost on me that this would be a book I would pick if I truly <b>WAS</b> stranded on an island. <br />1.For enjoyment purposes. <br />2.For tips on survival. Because who actually KNOWS how to make a fire? Me neither....<br />3.To hope and pray, that a doppelgänger of T.J. was living on the island with me.... <br /> <b>Enjoy that vision for a little while.....</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="2852094603412559355" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_547024505" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/547024505?book_show_action=true">Feb 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs">Amy | Foxy Blogs</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer547024505" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9308684727124608634"><b>Utterly breathtaking!</b><br/><br/>A friend of mine (Amy aka, Foxy) persuaded me to read this book and helped me through it since I was initially concerned about the subject matter. I couldn't be happier that she finally convinced me! If you are someone who, like me, tends to shy away from books involving sickness and/or tragedy, don't cross this one off your list; its focus lies on a very positive outcome and is substantially more encouraging than it is tragic. <br/><br/>Anna is T.J.'s tutor and agrees to attend a vac</span>
  <span id="freeText9308684727124608634" style="display:none"><b>Utterly breathtaking!</b><br><br>A friend of mine (Amy aka, Foxy) persuaded me to read this book and helped me through it since I was initially concerned about the subject matter. I couldn't be happier that she finally convinced me! If you are someone who, like me, tends to shy away from books involving sickness and/or tragedy, don't cross this one off your list; its focus lies on a very positive outcome and is substantially more encouraging than it is tragic. <br><br>Anna is T.J.'s tutor and agrees to attend a vacation with T.J. and his family in order to catch him up on school work during his summer break. When their plane goes down en route, Anna and T.J. become stranded on a desolate island with limited resources for survival. Together they face hardships, fatigue, sickness, and despair...as their hope for being rescued dwindles with time. But they also experience many triumphs, large and small—and those are what powerfully remain with me.<br><br>The extent of what these characters endured was as intense as it was encouraging. My heart broke at times, rejoiced during others, and never lost hope for the fate of T.J. and Anna. I'll admit to being slightly deterred by the considerable age difference; Anna being 30 and T.J., 16 when they first meet...but do not fret! Time passes, people mature, and I can assure you that all encounters are tasteful and very much 'legal'. The ultimate bond formed through despair was solid and heartwarming. <br><br>The pacing of this story is quick and flows gracefully. The monotony of being trapped on a deserted island could tend to make a story feel like its dragging— but this author tackles this feat flawlessly. I never once became bored; in fact, I found this to be a real page turner and extremely un-put-down-able!<br><br>It's amazing how one's view of life transforms when 'surviving' becomes the sole priority. It is then that you'll find all the unnecessary worries and petty desires stripped away, leaving behind only what truly matters in life...And I loved being able to witness this extraordinary and inspiring journey of survival. <br><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Contemporary Romance<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Moderate steam<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Beautiful, touching, slow-building connection. <br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Lovable and three-dementional. <br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> Centered on survival, and love conquering all hardship. <br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Accomplished, alluring, and knowledgable.<br><b>▪ POV:</b> First person: Alternating dual perspectives.<br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> None<br><b>▪	 Next Installment:</b> Novella: A story intertwining with this one. <br><b>▪ HEA? </b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1243050677" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1243050677" />
    <a title="Navessa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18104163-navessa"><img alt="Navessa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1444162983p2/18104163.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1243050677?book_show_action=true">Apr 01, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Navessa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Navessa" href="/user/show/18104163-navessa">Navessa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18104163-navessa?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1243050677" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17091360364214842617"><b>A lovely romance, an incredibly unique premise, but for me, parts of this fell flat.</b><br/><br/>It mostly comes down to what I expect from first person perspective. I expect emotion. I expect insight. Not only do I expect to read about a sequence of events, but I also expect to know what a character thinks and feels about those events as they unfold. <br/><br/>I didn't during most of this. <br/><br/>Imagine that you're stranded on an island in the middle of the Pacific, when suddenly your only companion and the person you happ</span>
  <span id="freeText17091360364214842617" style="display:none"><b>A lovely romance, an incredibly unique premise, but for me, parts of this fell flat.</b><br /><br />It mostly comes down to what I expect from first person perspective. I expect emotion. I expect insight. Not only do I expect to read about a sequence of events, but I also expect to know what a character thinks and feels about those events as they unfold. <br /><br />I didn't during most of this. <br /><br />Imagine that you're stranded on an island in the middle of the Pacific, when suddenly your only companion and the person you happen to love becomes violently ill out of nowhere:<br /><br /><i>"I found the first aid kit and shook two Tylenol into the palm of my hand. I helped him swallow the Tylenol with water, but he threw up all over himself a few minutes later. <br />I cleaned him up with a t-shirt and tried to shift him over a little, to a drier part of the blanket. He cried out when I touched him."</i><br /><br />That passage is one of many that left me wondering a lot of things. Is she freaking out because he's sick and all she has to treat him with is Tylenol? Did him puking turn her stomach? Isn't she terrified that the man she loves might die and there's nothing she can do to save him? <br /><br />TELL ME, DAMN IT!<br /><br />Okay, aside from my annoyance at the detached storytelling, there were other things missing from this. Things that won't bother most people, but things that nevertheless bothered the hell out of me. Because I used to live on a 8 x 5 mile tropical island. <br /><br />A huge part of what was lacking from this was the complete and overwhelming culture shock of returning to the mainland. How walking into a Walmart feels like tripping balls because the largest building you've seen in years was a mere fraction of its size. How being a passenger in a car going over 50 mph makes you have a panic attack because SLOW DOWN, YOU'RE GOING TO FUCKING KILL US. NO, I DON'T CARE THAT YOU'RE GOING THE SPEED LIMIT, HUMANS WERE NOT MEANT TO TRAVEL FASTER THAN A FART FLIES. <br /><br />So yeah, there's that. <br /><br />Honestly, I still think there's a lot of good in here. And I urge anyone looking for a unique love story to give this a try. <br /><br />Just don't read it on a plane. Because *shudder*<br /><br /><b><a href="http://www.thealliterates.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/thealliterates/" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/thealliterates" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/the_alliterates/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/thealliterates/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="17091360364214842617" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_548015920" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/548015920" />
    <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox"><img alt="Alex is The Romance Fox" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1428866380p2/6663962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/548015920?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex is The Romance Fox" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox">Alex is The Romance Fox</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101609095" href="/book/show/15506110-on-the-island">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=favorites-books">favorites-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=authors-a-h">authors-a-h</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=lendable">lendable</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer548015920" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9331521609382639277"><b> I LOVED IT!!!!</b><br/><br/>There have been so many amazing reviews written and by now everyone is familiar with the story-line and the characters. I could go on and on about this great love story but it would take pages and pages so I am just going to give a short version of my thoughts and feelings.<br/><br/>From the first paragraph - <br/><b>"I was thirty years old when the seaplane T.J. Callahan and I were traveling on crash-landed in the Indian Ocean. T.J. was sixteen, and three months into remission from Hodgkin's lymph</b></span>
  <span id="freeText9331521609382639277" style="display:none"><b> I LOVED IT!!!!</b><br /><br />There have been so many amazing reviews written and by now everyone is familiar with the story-line and the characters. I could go on and on about this great love story but it would take pages and pages so I am just going to give a short version of my thoughts and feelings.<br /><br />From the first paragraph - <br /><b>"I was thirty years old when the seaplane T.J. Callahan and I were traveling on crash-landed in the Indian Ocean. T.J. was sixteen, and three months into remission from Hodgkin's lymphoma. The pilot's name was Mick, but he died before we hit the water."</b><br />-I was captivated and found it impossible to stop until I reached the last page.<br /><br />The relationship build-up between Anna and TJ is just incredible and their interaction had me crying and then laughing……….<br /><br /><b>“[T.J.] I pulled my arms out from underneath her body and tucked her hair behind her ears. “I love you, Anna.”<br />The surprised look on her face told me she hadn't seen that coming.<br />“You weren't supposed to fall in love,” she whispered.<br />“Well, I did,” I said, looking into her eyes. “ I've been in love with you for months. I’m telling you now because I think you love me too, Anna. You just don’t think you’re supposed to. You’ll tell me when you’re ready. I can wait.” I pulled her mouth down to mine and kissed her and when it ended, I smiled and said, “Happy birthday.” <br /><br />“You named the chicken, Chicken?" <br />She looked embarrassed. "When we decided not to kill it, I got attached.”<br /><br />“[Anna] In February, I woke up from a nap. A bouquet of flowers gathered from the various bushes and shrubs scattered around the island lay on the blanket beside me, a small length of rope wound around their stems.<br />I found T.J. down at the shore. “Someone’s been checking the calendar.”<br />He grinned. “I didn't want to miss Valentine’s Day.”<br />I kissed him. “You’re sweet to me.”<br />Pulling me closer, he said, “It’s not hard, Anna.”<br />I stared into T.J.’s eyes, and he started to sway. My arms went around his neck and we danced, moving in a circle, the sand soft and warm under our feet.<br />“You don’t need music, do you?”<br />“No,” T.J. said. “But I do need you.</b><br /><br />The plot, the endearing and unforgettable characters, the build-up is really awesome….so real and so believable. I loved that the story is told in Anna &amp; TJ’s POV. <br /><br /><b>“I never wanted anyone else, T.J. I just wanted what was best for you."<br />"You are what's best for me," he said, cradling my head in his arms, his legs intertwined with mine. "I'm not going anywhere, Anna. This is right where I want to be.” </b><br /><br />And I liked the fact that their story happens over a long period of time, giving us a real in-depth look into what they feel – the fear, the hope of survival, love and the struggles they endure both on the island and when they return home. I felt those feelings with them and at times I felt so happy and others so dam sad. I wanted them to succeed, to be together, and to find happiness. <br /><br />I learnt so much from this story – that anything is possible if you just open up and let it in. <br /><br />My favorite quote in this book says it so well – all the possibilities in life!!!!<br /><br /><b>“I don’t fit in your world.”<br />“Neither do I,” he said, his expression tender yet resolute. “So let’s make our own. We've done it before.”</b><br /><br />A truly remarkable debut novel and wow….can‘t wait for the movie!!!!!!!!!!!!<br /><br />This has become one of my favorite books of all time – I am so glad I discovered this author and this book!!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9331521609382639277" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1521027680" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17588470951633356132">Story Rating ~ 5 HUGE STARS!<br/>Hero Rating ~ 5 STARS!<br/>Heroine Rating ~ 5 STARS!<br/>Romance Rating ~ 5 STARS!<br/>Heat Level ~ 3 Stars<br/>Ending ~ 5 STARS!<br/>Overall Rating ~ 5 NOW THAT WAS AN AMAZING READ STARS!<br/><br/>This is one of those books, you know the one that has been sitting on your ereader, the one you were planning to read but just never got around to it. After reading Auntee’s review for the second time around, I finally decided that it’s time I get down to it and I gave this book a go, I’m SO glad I finally d</span>
  <span id="freeText17588470951633356132" style="display:none">Story Rating ~ 5 HUGE STARS!<br />Hero Rating ~ 5 STARS!<br />Heroine Rating ~ 5 STARS!<br />Romance Rating ~ 5 STARS!<br />Heat Level ~ 3 Stars<br />Ending ~ 5 STARS!<br />Overall Rating ~ 5 NOW THAT WAS AN AMAZING READ STARS!<br /><br />This is one of those books, you know the one that has been sitting on your ereader, the one you were planning to read but just never got around to it. After reading Auntee’s review for the second time around, I finally decided that it’s time I get down to it and I gave this book a go, I’m SO glad I finally did.<br /><br />This was an AMAZING read about an older woman and a teenage boy getting stranded on an Island together. I was hooked in big time reading about how they lived day to day, how they managed finding food and water plus making fire and building shelter. These two made a perfect team, they needed each other in order to survive. They took care of each other when illnesses set in, each knowing that if one of them died the other one eventually would too.<br /><br />As years passed on the Island, our hero T.J. went from being a teenager to becoming a man and along with that, Anna and T.J.’s feelings for each other grew deeper. The love they shared for each other was so very lovely, nothing felt out of place for me even though he was 14 years younger than her. The love scenes were beautifully written with such passion and class and did not take place until T.J. was almost 19. <br /><br />Just when they were about ready to give up hope of ever being found, a bad storm rolled in almost taking the lives of T.J. and Anna. This is when they finally get rescued. <br />Once T.J and Anna are back home, they have to deal with their age difference. They both had insecurities to work out and this took a bit of time but through it all, their love for each other was always there.<br /><br />I do not recommend books too often, but this is one of those books that if you are interested in reading, DON’T WAIT! Make it your next read and enjoy this wonderful adventure. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17588470951633356132" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_402816963" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/402816963" />
    <a title="Steelwhisper" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7962895-steelwhisper"><img alt="Steelwhisper" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1373520142p2/7962895.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/402816963?book_show_action=true">Aug 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Steelwhisper" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Steelwhisper" href="/user/show/7962895-steelwhisper">Steelwhisper</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/12586192-on-the-island">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7962895-steelwhisper?shelf=1-bad">1-bad</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7962895-steelwhisper?shelf=boring">boring</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7962895-steelwhisper?shelf=m-f">m-f</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7962895-steelwhisper?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7962895-steelwhisper?shelf=sexuality">sexuality</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7962895-steelwhisper?shelf=love">love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7962895-steelwhisper?shelf=hero-heroine-tstl">hero-heroine-tstl</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7962895-steelwhisper?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer402816963" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7593190461758492375">It's not easy for me to give this 1* only and I've thought about this long and hard. Normally I would have either not rated this at all, or given it a 2* and shrugged. However, I am a bit too angry about the way this was written for comfort and a shrug. So allow me to explain...<br/><br/>(there may be spoilers)<br/><br/>I was prepared to like this and--quite unlike American readers--I live in a country where 16 is the age of consent, even for relationships between much older adults and youths, and Anne's alleged po</span>
  <span id="freeText7593190461758492375" style="display:none">It's not easy for me to give this 1* only and I've thought about this long and hard. Normally I would have either not rated this at all, or given it a 2* and shrugged. However, I am a bit too angry about the way this was written for comfort and a shrug. So allow me to explain...<br /><br />(there may be spoilers)<br /><br />I was prepared to like this and--quite unlike American readers--I live in a country where 16 is the age of consent, even for relationships between much older adults and youths, and Anne's alleged post as a teacher in my opinion never truly floated. They crashed before she took up teaching him and there was no activity as a teacher either on the island. I didn't mind the age aspect at all, in fact I read the book for it, because I wanted to read a well-written book about just such an age-gap.<br /><br />I'm not going into the numerous problems I had with basic writing skills I expect from a book, such as are relative to grammar, punctuation and style. Or that I'd expect the stream of consciousness from two people that apart in gender, experience and age to be at least somewhat different and not uniformly juvenile. I do have much more problems with the story however.<br /><br />Let me state it clearly: any female shaving her legs, underarms and pits, hung up to the point of ridiculousness about natural body odours and wildly applying hair conditioner as well as being crazy about recovering a suitcase filled with beauty items while stranded on a tropical island has to have her head examined. From that moment onwards I lost every shred of respect for this female character. <br /><br />Just as it rather soon started to grate on me that neither Anne, nor TJ ever had any even halfway deep conversation or addressed any of the obvious problems bound to arise between them. I had trouble believing in the aliveness and reality of both of them. TJ was too good to be true, and stayed that way, and Anne came over as shallow and immature despite all her protestations to the contrary.<br /><br />The romance felt contrived, there was no build-up, Anne being too prude to even contemplate the topic realistically until the last moment and TJ is suddenly the big seducer and superb lover quite out of the blue. Anyone who had hoped for even a tiny bit of sensuality or on-screen sex will be disappointed by the way. This book is practically sex-free, even though going by the blurb you're led to believe it's one of the main topics. <br /><br />What truly enervated me though was the moralising. You might expect some openmindedness from a book about a reversed May-December couple, but what liberal view at this topic there was, was mere window-dressing. It felt as forced as the turn of the heroine towards dogoodieness, while the real message below the alleged liberalism was 1) women have to have (lots) of babies, and 2) people just have to marry, then whatever they do is acceptable. Yes. That. <br /><br />Nowhere were the real issues of an age-gap relationship truly taken up, even the people who were critical still behaved with a restraint I found entirely unbelievable and things proceeded too smoothly just about in every respect. After the candyfloss HEA with a marriage, multiple babies (of course the 15 y/o TJ had his semen frozen) and everybody's problem nicely solved and tucked safely into a cozy bed, I was left gnashing my teeth.<br /><br />This story idea had a lot going for it, but it sure has been turned into one of the soppiest and most sugar-coated romances I read, ever. The 1* is exclusively for the excellent idea and the one or two times I laughed out loud over some particularly funny faux pas.<br /><br />I can't recommend this. Especially not if someone looks for a well-written story about an age-gap couple!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7593190461758492375" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_353170080" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/353170080" />
    <a title="Jill" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3820197-jill"><img alt="Jill" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1383385041p2/3820197.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/353170080?book_show_action=true">Jun 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jill" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jill" href="/user/show/3820197-jill">Jill</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781101609095" href="/book/show/15506110-on-the-island">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3820197-jill?shelf=2012-debuts">2012-debuts</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3820197-jill?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3820197-jill?shelf=2012-4-5-5-stars">2012-4-5-5-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer353170080" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4428667218811716596"><br/><b> 4.5 stars</b><br/><br/><i>I was thirty years old when the seaplane T.J. Callahan and I were traveling on crash-landed in the Indian Ocean. T.J. was sixteen...</i><br/><br/>Treatment for cancer has left T.J. behind in his studies. His parents hire teacher Anna Emerson to tutor T.J. over the summer at their rental on one of the small islands off the main island of the Maldives. When the pilot suffers a fatal heart attack, the seaplane crashes into the ocean and T.J. and Anna make it to a small, uninhabited island.<br/><br/>To pare down </span>
  <span id="freeText4428667218811716596" style="display:none"><br /><b> 4.5 stars</b><br /><br /><i>I was thirty years old when the seaplane T.J. Callahan and I were traveling on crash-landed in the Indian Ocean. T.J. was sixteen...</i><br /><br />Treatment for cancer has left T.J. behind in his studies. His parents hire teacher Anna Emerson to tutor T.J. over the summer at their rental on one of the small islands off the main island of the Maldives. When the pilot suffers a fatal heart attack, the seaplane crashes into the ocean and T.J. and Anna make it to a small, uninhabited island.<br /><br />To pare down a story to its bones - hero, heroine, small island - and manage to keep the plot interesting, without slowing the pacing to a crawl, is remarkable and indicative of the talent of this author. The plot is simple. The characterisations realistic. The pacing subdued. Told from both T.J. and Anna's first-person points-of-view, this is a quite beautiful love story.<br /><br />The relationship is written realistically. Their growth from teacher/student to friends to lovers is incremental. Watching them slowly, plausibly fall for each other is the heart of this story. Handled tactfully, this novel raises none of the concerns at the inherently inappropriate relationship between a thirty year-old woman and a teenager. Their sexual relationship begins when T.J. is in every sense a man, though a few months shy of his nineteenth birthday. Having first beaten cancer, a plane crash and now the rigours of island survival, T.J. has matured beyond his years.<br /><br />While on the island this was a near perfect read for me. When they arrived back to civilisation it fell apart slightly. The ending though, was sweet fulfilment.<br /><br />A beautiful romance and an impressive debut.<br /><br /><b>Steam:</b> 2.5<br /><br /><i>ARC courtesy of Penguin (Australia) via NetGalley</i><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4428667218811716596" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer383415421" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10338965574102216020">I started this book thinking<br/><br/><i>'Ah, seems like a weird book with a huge age gap beween the main leads and the story seems like its going to be dragged'</i><br/><br/><u>Holy hell, how wrong was I.</u><br/><br/>God fucking knows why I haven't read this book when I've had it since like Aug '12!!   <span id="freeText10338965574102216020" style="display:none">I started this book thinking<br><br><i>'Ah, seems like a weird book with a huge age gap beween the main leads and the story seems like its going to be dragged'</i><br><br><u>Holy hell, how wrong was I.</u><br><br>God fucking knows why I haven't read this book when I've had it since like Aug '12!! I feel like kicking myself, HARD!!<br><br><b>Author, I love you and I've got only one thing to say to you</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386336i/745783.png" width="240" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380386337ra/745784.gif" width="340" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>^ ^ ^ I was like this after finishing the book. ^ ^ ^<br><br><b>I AM TOTALLY IN LOVE WITH THIS BOOK</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380386337ra/745785.gif" width="240" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Totally touch me to the core</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380386337ra/745786.gif" width="340" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>My eyes should really stop leaking now, but I'm just tooooo moved by this incredible book</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380386337ra/745787.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>When I reached 58% of the book, I yelped, jumped around like a mad child and ran into my hall where my mother was sitting and screamed "FOUND THEM" and she thought I was absolutely nuts, but she knew what I was talking about because as I was reading this book, I keep telling her about it and gushing about the absolutely amazing story I'm reading.   <b>What an AMAZING book, Its like a totally must read.</b>
</u><br>The way the author has written this book, its capturing. I didn't put it down for a minute. Both the main characters were like the best and totally priceless! I loved/adored them! Seriously, I'm smittened to the core by this book. T.J and Anna were PREFECT! Their love so pure, the 13/14year age gap was barely noticed. Their whole journey, their experience was so capturing I was in awe of the book.<br>Each scene was so capturing and it portrayed so many emotions, each twist and turn left me totally stunned and the only though processing in my brain was WOW!! THIS BOOK IS SOMETHING ELSE IN THIS OWN LEAGUE!!<br>Each twist they over came, I felt a rush of emotions, I felt fear for them, love for them, I felt proud of them for surviving and I felt honor for them, I am like a mixture of toooo many emotions! I am so overwhelmed!<br><br>After some of the most intese scenes, the author would lighten the mood by a good line or an excellent scene<br><br><i>Dinner was always special when you killed it, instead of the other way around.</i><br><br><i>“What’s it like being with her? Is it true what they say about older chicks?”<br>“She’s not that much older.”<br>“Uh, okay. So anyway, how is it?”<br>“It’s incredible.”<br>“What’s she do?”<br>“She does everything, Ben.”</i><br><br>~<br><br><b>Please, Read this book if you haven't! It is sooo worth it!</b></span>

However, my own rating sat at 3.5 Stars all these years so I decided to give it a re-do in order to find out WTF was going on. Turns out I either suffered a concussion or wasn’t prepared to embrace my inner whore back in the day because I. MOTHEREFFING. LOVE. THIS. STORY. The synopsis and all that mumbo jumbo are contained in my original review below so I’m not going to bother rehashing the plot. All I will say is that I GOTTA POCKET GOTTA POCKET FULL OF SUNSHINE!!!!!!!!!!!!!<br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I hope I haven't been lying to myself : (<br><br><br><b>ORIGINAL REVIEW:</b> <br><br>17-year old T.J. is in remission after battling cancer. His mother has decided to celebrate by having the entire family spend the summer in the Maldives and has headed there early with the rest of the family. T.J. does not share his mother’s excitement (especially after learning 30-year old teacher Anna will be tagging along as a tutor to get him up to speed with his schoolwork) and sought a few day reprieve from the vacation by staying in Chicago. He and Anna are en route to the vacation home when the pilot of the seaplane they are on suffers a fatal heart attack and crash lands in the middle of the Indian Ocean. They make it to one of hundreds in a string of inhabited islands, but how will two city dwellers ever survive living on a deserted island?<br><br>I will gladly admit one of my earliest guilty pleasures was “The Blue Lagoon”. It was so awful and campy, but I just looooooved it so when this popped up on the radar in the middle of July, I was all in. This book brought back all of those old feelings and was the perfect summer read. I was prepared for it to be all porn-y and get squicked out by the age difference of T.J. and Anna, but it wasn’t like that at all (a pleasant surprise). Recommended to anyone who wants to read a better-than-average romance novel and escape for a day or so.<br></span>

<div id="review_676364580" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=new-adult-express">new-adult-express</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=contemporary-duckie">contemporary-duckie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-love-my-friends">i-love-my-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=oops-let-s-do-it-again-romance">oops-let-s-do-it-again-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=third-time-s-the-charm-romance">third-time-s-the-charm-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=special-and-precious">special-and-precious</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer676364580" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7149665555564281295"><b>5 STARS!!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397592706i/9297960._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This is my second time reading it and loved it even more than the first time around! Wow, just simply amazeballs!<br/><br/>This is a book where the blurb <i>jumped</i> out to me. A much older female tutor and an in-remission teenager crash in the ocean and end up on a deserted island? Well sign me up! A very realistic, heartwarming, and thought-provoking read, <u>On the Island</u> will always remain a top favorite on my shelf!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397592706i/9297961._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The story is told from dual POVs. Enter Anna, a 30 year old English teacher who is h</span>
  <span id="freeText7149665555564281295" style="display:none"><b>5 STARS!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397592706i/9297960._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is my second time reading it and loved it even more than the first time around! Wow, just simply amazeballs!<br><br>This is a book where the blurb <i>jumped</i> out to me. A much older female tutor and an in-remission teenager crash in the ocean and end up on a deserted island? Well sign me up! A very realistic, heartwarming, and thought-provoking read, <u>On the Island</u> will always remain a top favorite on my shelf!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397592706i/9297961._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story is told from dual POVs. Enter Anna, a 30 year old English teacher who is hired to tutor T.J. all summer in the Maldives. Anna is such a well-rounded character: she’s gorgeous, sophisticated, and knows what she wants in life. However, she isn’t too satisfied in her current relationship with her longtime boyfriend John, another minor reason to accept the summer tutoring job to get away, relax, and process. As level-headed and calm as she is, Anna couldn’t have known that in just hours, she and T.J. would land head-first in the Indian Ocean after their charter plan crashes. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397592706i/9297962._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Simply put, T.J. is an amazing character! At the beginning of the story, he’s an almost seventeen year old dreading the idea of spending the summer with his family and studying when all he wants to do is hang out with friends. What really made him stand out is that despite his young age, he’s such a mature guy. His battle with cancer really put his life into perspective: while others his age are out partying and getting laid, he goes through treatments, banks his sperm, and goes through a significant amount of chemo. Usually I shy away from books that bring in the cancer aspect since I think it’s an overused trope in stories, but this author realistically and expertly weaves this element into the book. <br><br>The part that really spoke out to me, however, was the nature of T.J. and Anna’s relationship and how it smoothly progressed from acquaintances to lovers. I totally dig anything taboo and forbidden and at first glance, that’s exactly what T.J. and Anna’s relationship is viewed as – she’s 30 and he’s 16. However, when they finally are together as a couple, everything is very much legal and with the amount of time that passes while they’re on the island, both characters mature in age and mind so their encounters were very believable and expected. I have no doubt in my mind that if T.J. and Anna didn’t land up on their island, they probably wouldn’t have ended up pursing a relationship together; however, some things in life happen unexpectedly and it’s unfortunate they got dished this plate. It’s amazing that when survival is at the forefront of your mind, meaningless worries are stripped away and what’s left behind is what and <i>who</i> really matters. Age ceases to be an issue. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397592706i/9297963._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, a beautifully-written, inspirational, and unconventional tale of love, life, and survival that I’d recommend everyone to read! Don’t let the taboo and subject matter deter you from picking up this unique story; it’s definitely worth the read (and re-read). <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="7149665555564281295" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>
